      style='FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Georgia",serif; LAYOUT-GRID-MODE: line; mso-bidi-font-family: PMingLiU; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体'>2. 
      </SPAN><B><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LAYOUT-GRID-MODE: line; mso-bidi-font-family: PMingLiU; mso-ascii-font-family: Georgia; mso-hansi-font-family: Georgia">所占权益及长期购电容量和购电安排</SPAN></B><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LAYOUT-GRID-MODE: line; mso-bidi-font-family: PMingLiU; mso-ascii-font-family: Georgia; mso-hansi-font-family: Georgia">即除上述（</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-GB 
      style='FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Georgia",serif; LAYOUT-GRID-MODE: line; mso-bidi-font-family: PMingLiU; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LAYOUT-GRID-MODE: line; mso-bidi-font-family: PMingLiU; mso-ascii-font-family: Georgia; mso-hansi-font-family: Georgia">）项外，也包括中电为满足客户需求而购买的额外容量和电量的集团发电和及储能组合，并符合以下条件：</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-GB 
      style='FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Georgia",serif; LAYOUT-GRID-MODE: line; mso-bidi-font-family: PMingLiU; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体'><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
      <P class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 16.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: normal; TEXT-INDENT: -14.15pt; mso-add-space: auto; mso-list: l3 level1 lfo4"><SPAN

      </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-GB 
      style='FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Georgia",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: Calibri; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-language: EN-US'>Nuclear<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>

<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 8pt"><SPAN lang=EN-GB 
style='FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Georgia",serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: Helv; mso-fareast-font-family: "等线 Light"; mso-fareast-theme-font: major-fareast'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: normal; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><SPAN 
lang=EN-GB 
style='FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Georgia",serif; COLOR: black; mso-bidi-font-family: Helv; mso-fareast-font-family: "等线 Light"; mso-fareast-theme-font: major-fareast'>Our 
assurance was with respect to the year ended 31 December 2020 information only 
and we have not performed any procedures with respect to earlier periods or any 
other elements included in the 2020 Sustainability Report and, therefore, do not 
express any conclusion thereon.<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: normal; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><SPAN 
lang=EN-GB 
style='FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Georgia",serif; COLOR: black; mso-bidi-font-family: Helv; mso-fareast-font-family: "等线 Light"; mso-fareast-theme-font: major-fareast'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: normal; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><B><SPAN 
lang=EN-GB 
style='FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Georgia",serif; COLOR: black; mso-bidi-font-family: Helv; mso-fareast-font-family: "等线 Light"; mso-fareast-theme-font: major-fareast'>Criteria<o:p></o:p></SPAN></B></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: normal; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><SPAN 
lang=EN-GB 
style='FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Georgia",serif; COLOR: black; mso-bidi-font-family: Helv; mso-fareast-font-family: "等线 Light"; mso-fareast-theme-font: major-fareast'>The 
criteria used by the Company to prepare the Identified Sustainability 
Information is set out in the Reporting scope and data verification (the 
“Criteria”) (Appendix II) appended to this report.<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: normal; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><SPAN 
lang=EN-GB 
style='FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Georgia",serif; COLOR: black; mso-bidi-font-family: Helv; mso-fareast-font-family: "等线 Light"; mso-fareast-theme-font: major-fareast'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: normal; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><B><SPAN 
lang=EN-GB 
style='FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Georgia",serif; COLOR: black; mso-bidi-font-family: Helv; mso-fareast-font-family: "等线 Light"; mso-fareast-theme-font: major-fareast'>The 
Company’s Responsibility for the Identified Sustainability 
Information<o:p></o:p></SPAN></B></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: normal; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><SPAN 
lang=EN-GB 
style='FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Georgia",serif; COLOR: black; mso-bidi-font-family: Helv; mso-fareast-font-family: "等线 Light"; mso-fareast-theme-font: major-fareast'>The 
Company is responsible for the preparation of the Identified Sustainability 
Information in accordance with the Criteria. This responsibility includes the 
design, implementation and maintenance of internal control relevant to the 
preparation of Identified Sustainability Information that is free from material 
misstatement, whether due to fraud or error.<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: normal; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><SPAN 
lang=EN-GB 
style='FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Georgia",serif; COLOR: black; mso-bidi-font-family: Helv; mso-fareast-font-family: "等线 Light"; mso-fareast-theme-font: major-fareast'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: normal; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><B><SPAN 
lang=EN-GB 
style='FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Georgia",serif; COLOR: black; mso-bidi-font-family: Helv; mso-fareast-font-family: "等线 Light"; mso-fareast-theme-font: major-fareast'>Inherent 
limitations<o:p></o:p></SPAN></B></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: normal; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><SPAN 
lang=EN-GB 
style='FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Georgia",serif; COLOR: black; mso-bidi-font-family: Helv; mso-fareast-font-family: "等线 Light"; mso-fareast-theme-font: major-fareast'>The 
absence of a significant body of established practice on which to draw to 
evaluate and measure non- financial information allows for different, but 
acceptable, measures and measurement techniques and can affect comparability 
between entities. In addition, greenhouse gas (“GHG”) quantification is subject 
to inherent uncertainty because of incomplete scientific knowledge used to 
determine emissions factors and the values needed to combine emissions of 
different gases.<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: normal; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><SPAN 
lang=EN-GB 
style='FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Georgia",serif; COLOR: black; mso-bidi-font-family: Helv; mso-fareast-font-family: "等线 Light"; mso-fareast-theme-font: major-fareast'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: normal; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><B><SPAN 
lang=EN-GB 
style='FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Georgia",serif; COLOR: black; mso-bidi-font-family: Helv; mso-fareast-font-family: "等线 Light"; mso-fareast-theme-font: major-fareast'>Our 
Independence and Quality Control<o:p></o:p></SPAN></B></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: normal; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><SPAN 
lang=EN-GB 
style='FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Georgia",serif; COLOR: black; mso-bidi-font-family: Helv; mso-fareast-font-family: "等线 Light"; mso-fareast-theme-font: major-fareast'>We 
have complied with the independence and other ethical requirements of the Code 
of Ethics for Professional Accountants issued by the International Ethics 
Standards Board for Accountants, which is founded on fundamental principles of 
integrity, objectivity, professional competence and due care, confidentiality 
and professional behaviour.<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: normal; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><SPAN 
lang=EN-GB 
style='FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Georgia",serif; COLOR: black; mso-bidi-font-family: Helv; mso-fareast-font-family: "等线 Light"; mso-fareast-theme-font: major-fareast'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: normal; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><SPAN 
lang=EN-GB 
style='FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Georgia",serif; COLOR: black; mso-bidi-font-family: Helv; mso-fareast-font-family: "等线 Light"; mso-fareast-theme-font: major-fareast'>Our 
firm applies International Standard on Quality Control 1 and accordingly 
maintains a comprehensive system of quality control including documented 
policies and procedures regarding compliance with ethical requirements, 
professional standards and applicable legal and regulatory 
requirements.<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: normal; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><SPAN 
lang=EN-GB 
style='FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Georgia",serif; COLOR: black; mso-bidi-font-family: Helv; mso-fareast-font-family: "等线 Light"; mso-fareast-theme-font: major-fareast'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: normal; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><B><SPAN 
lang=EN-GB 
style='FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Georgia",serif; COLOR: black; mso-bidi-font-family: Helv; mso-fareast-font-family: "等线 Light"; mso-fareast-theme-font: major-fareast'>Our 
Responsibility<o:p></o:p></SPAN></B></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: normal; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><SPAN 
lang=EN-GB 
style='FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Georgia",serif; COLOR: black; mso-bidi-font-family: Helv; mso-fareast-font-family: "等线 Light"; mso-fareast-theme-font: major-fareast'>Our 
responsibility is to express a limited assurance conclusion on the Identified 
Sustainability Information based on the procedures we have performed and the 
evidence we have obtained. We conducted our limited assurance engagement in 
accordance with International Standard on Assurance Engagements 3000 (Revised), 
Assurance Engagements other than Audits or Reviews of Historical Financial 
Information, and, in respect of greenhouse gas emissions, International Standard 
on Assurance Engagements 3410, Assurance Engagements on Greenhouse Gas 
Statements, issued by the International Auditing and Assurance Standards Board. 
These standards require that we plan and perform this engagement to obtain 
limited assurance about whether the Identified Sustainability Information is 
free from material misstatement.<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: normal; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><SPAN 
lang=EN-GB 
style='FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Georgia",serif; COLOR: black; mso-bidi-font-family: Helv; mso-fareast-font-family: "等线 Light"; mso-fareast-theme-font: major-fareast'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: normal; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><SPAN 
lang=EN-GB 
style='FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Georgia",serif; COLOR: black; mso-bidi-font-family: Helv; mso-fareast-font-family: "等线 Light"; mso-fareast-theme-font: major-fareast'>A 
limited assurance engagement involves assessing the suitability in the 
circumstances of the Company’s use of the Criteria as the basis for the 
preparation of the Identified Sustainability Information, assessing the risks of 
material misstatement of the Identified Sustainability Information whether due 
to fraud or error, responding to the assessed risks as necessary in the 
circumstances, and evaluating the overall presentation of the Identified 
Sustainability Information. A limited assurance engagement is substantially less 
in scope than a reasonable assurance engagement in relation to both the risk 
assessment procedures, including an understanding of internal control, and the 
procedures performed in response to the assessed risks.<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: normal; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><SPAN 
lang=EN-GB 
style='FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Georgia",serif; COLOR: black; mso-bidi-font-family: Helv; mso-fareast-font-family: "等线 Light"; mso-fareast-theme-font: major-fareast'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></SPAN></P><SPAN 
lang=EN-GB 
style='FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Georgia",serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: Helv; mso-fareast-font-family: "等线 Light"; mso-fareast-theme-font: major-fareast; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-ansi-language: EN-GB; mso-bidi-language: AR-SA'><BR 
style="PAGE-BREAK-BEFORE: always; mso-special-character: line-break" 
clear=all></SPAN>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 8pt"><SPAN lang=EN-GB 
style='FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Georgia",serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: Helv; mso-fareast-font-family: "等线 Light"; mso-fareast-theme-font: major-fareast'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: normal; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><SPAN 
lang=EN-GB 
style='FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Georgia",serif; COLOR: black; mso-bidi-font-family: Helv; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体'>The 
procedures we performed were based on our professional judgment and included 
inquiries, observation of processes performed, inspection of documents, 
analytical procedures, evaluating the appropriateness of quantification methods 
and reporting policies, and agreeing or reconciling with underlying 
records.<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: normal; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><SPAN 
lang=EN-GB 
style='FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Georgia",serif; COLOR: black; mso-bidi-font-family: Helv; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: normal; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><SPAN 
lang=EN-GB 
style='FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Georgia",serif; COLOR: black; mso-bidi-font-family: Helv; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体'>Given 
the circumstances of the engagement, in performing the procedures listed above 
we:<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: normal; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><SPAN 
lang=EN-GB 
style='FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Georgia",serif; COLOR: black; mso-bidi-font-family: Helv; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: normal; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ; TEXT-INDENT: -21.3pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-add-space: auto; mso-list: l7 level1 lfo6"><SPAN 
lang=EN-GB 
style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Symbol; COLOR: black; mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol; mso-fareast-font-family: Symbol"><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">·<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-GB 
style='FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Georgia",serif; COLOR: black; mso-bidi-font-family: Helv; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体'>made 
inquiries of the persons responsible for the Identified Sustainability 
Information;<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: normal; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ; TEXT-INDENT: -21.3pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-add-space: auto; mso-list: l7 level1 lfo6"><SPAN 
lang=EN-GB 
style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Symbol; COLOR: black; mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol; mso-fareast-font-family: Symbol"><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">·<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-GB 
style='FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Georgia",serif; COLOR: black; mso-bidi-font-family: Helv; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体'>understood 
the process for collecting and reporting the Identified Sustainability 
Information;<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: normal; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ; TEXT-INDENT: -21.3pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-add-space: auto; mso-list: l7 level1 lfo6"><SPAN 
lang=EN-GB 
style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Symbol; COLOR: black; mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol; mso-fareast-font-family: Symbol"><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">·<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-GB 
style='FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Georgia",serif; COLOR: black; mso-bidi-font-family: Helv; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体'>performed 
limited substantive testing on a selective basis of the Identified 
Sustainability Information; and<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: normal; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ; TEXT-INDENT: -21.3pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-add-space: auto; mso-list: l7 level1 lfo6"><SPAN 
lang=EN-GB 
style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Symbol; COLOR: black; mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol; mso-fareast-font-family: Symbol"><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">·<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-GB 
style='FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Georgia",serif; COLOR: black; mso-bidi-font-family: Helv; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体'>considered 
the disclosure and presentation of the Identified Sustainability 
Information.<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: normal; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><SPAN 
lang=EN-GB 
style='FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Georgia",serif; COLOR: black; mso-bidi-font-family: Helv; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: normal; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><SPAN 
lang=EN-GB 
style='FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Georgia",serif; COLOR: black; mso-bidi-font-family: Helv; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体'>The 
procedures performed in a limited assurance engagement vary in nature and timing 
from, and are less in extent than for, a reasonable assurance engagement. 
Consequently, the level of assurance obtained in a limited assurance engagement 
is substantially lower than the assurance that would have been obtained had we 
performed a reasonable assurance engagement. Accordingly, we do not express a 
reasonable assurance opinion about whether the Company’s Identified 
Sustainability Information has been prepared, in all material respects, in 
accordance with the Criteria.<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: normal; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><SPAN 
lang=EN-GB 
style='FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Georgia",serif; COLOR: black; mso-bidi-font-family: Helv; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: normal; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><B><SPAN 
lang=EN-GB 
style='FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Georgia",serif; COLOR: black; mso-bidi-font-family: Helv; mso-fareast-font-family: "等线 Light"; mso-fareast-theme-font: major-fareast'>Limited 
Assurance Conclusion<o:p></o:p></SPAN></B></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: normal; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><SPAN 
lang=EN-GB 
style='FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Georgia",serif; COLOR: black; mso-bidi-font-family: Helv; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体'>Based 
on the procedures we have performed and the evidence we have obtained, nothing 
has come to our attention that causes us to believe that the Company’s 
Identified Sustainability Information for the year ended 31 December 2020 is not 
prepared, in all material respects, in accordance with the 
Criteria.<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: normal; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><SPAN 
lang=EN-GB 
style='FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Georgia",serif; COLOR: black; mso-bidi-font-family: Helv; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal

lang=EN-GB 
style='FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Georgia",serif; COLOR: black; mso-bidi-font-family: Helv; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体'>Our 
report has been prepared for and only for the board of directors of CLP Holdings 
Limited and for no other purpose. We do not assume responsibility towards or 
accept liability to any other person for the content of this 
report.<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>

      3 CO2e<o:p></o:p></SPAN></B></P>

      indirect emissions (not included in Scope 2) that occur in the value chain

      <P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: normal"><SPAN 
      lang=EN-GB 
      style='FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Georgia",serif; LAYOUT-GRID-MODE: line; mso-bidi-font-family: PMingLiU; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="mso-yfti-irow: 1">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; BORDER-RIGHT: black 1pt solid; WIDTH: 97.55pt; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-top-alt: solid black .5pt; mso-border-top-themecolor: text1; mso-border-bottom-themecolor: text1; mso-border-right-themecolor: text1; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid black .5pt; mso-border-right-alt: solid black .5pt"

      <P class=MsoNormal

      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: normal"><B><SPAN lang=EN-GB

      <P class=MsoNormal

      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: normal"><B><SPAN lang=EN-GB

      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: normal"><B><SPAN lang=EN-GB

      on an equity/ an equity plus long-term capacity and energy purchase 
      basis)</SPAN></B><SPAN lang=EN-GB 
      style='FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Georgia",serif; LAYOUT-GRID-MODE: line; mso-bidi-font-family: PMingLiU; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体'><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P></TD>
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; BORDER-RIGHT: #f0f0f0; WIDTH: 328.55pt; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-left-alt: solid black .5pt; mso-border-left-themecolor: text1; mso-border-top-alt: solid black .5pt; mso-border-top-themecolor: text1; mso-border-bottom-themecolor: text1; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid black .5pt"

      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: normal"><SPAN 
      lang=EN-GB 
      style='FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Georgia",serif; LAYOUT-GRID-MODE: line; mso-bidi-font-family: PMingLiU; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体'>Data 
      are consolidated on an equity basis with two 
      variations:<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
      <P class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 15.95pt; LINE-HEIGHT: normal; TEXT-INDENT: -15.95pt; mso-add-space: auto; mso-list: l4 level1 lfo8"><SPAN 
      lang=EN-GB

      style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
      </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><B><SPAN lang=EN-GB 
      style='FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Georgia",serif; LAYOUT-GRID-MODE: line; mso-bidi-font-family: PMingLiU; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体'>Equity 
      basis</SPAN></B><SPAN lang=EN-GB 
      style='FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Georgia",serif; LAYOUT-GRID-MODE: line; mso-bidi-font-family: PMingLiU; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体'> 
      includes the assets in the Group’s generation and energy storage portfolio 
      that are:<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
      <P class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 15.95pt; LINE-HEIGHT: normal; TEXT-INDENT: -15.95pt; mso-add-space: auto; mso-list: l2 level1 lfo7"><SPAN 
      lang=EN-GB 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Symbol; LAYOUT-GRID-MODE: line; mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol; mso-fareast-font-family: Symbol"><SPAN

      </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-GB 
      style='FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Georgia",serif; LAYOUT-GRID-MODE: line; mso-bidi-font-family: PMingLiU; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体'>Owned 
      by CLP, where assets are included on an equity basis (i.e. accounts for 
      the data according to CLP’s equity share in the asset); 
      and<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
      <P class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 15.95pt; LINE-HEIGHT: normal; TEXT-INDENT: -15.95pt; mso-add-space: auto; mso-list: l2 level1 lfo7"><SPAN

      operation during the reporting year.<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
      <P class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 15.95pt; LINE-HEIGHT: normal; TEXT-INDENT: -15.95pt; mso-add-space: auto; mso-list: l4 level1 lfo8"><SPAN

      style='FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Georgia",serif; LAYOUT-GRID-MODE: line; mso-bidi-font-family: PMingLiU; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体'>Equity 
      plus long-term capacity and energy purchase basis </SPAN></B><SPAN 
      lang=EN-GB 
      style='FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Georgia",serif; LAYOUT-GRID-MODE: line; mso-bidi-font-family: PMingLiU; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体'>adds 
      onto (1) above and includes the assets in the Group’s generation and

      meet customer demand, and where:<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>

      style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 15.95pt; LINE-HEIGHT: normal; TEXT-INDENT: -15.95pt; mso-add-space: auto; mso-list: l2 level1 lfo7"><SPAN

      agreement duration is at least 5 years; and<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
      <P class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 15.95pt; LINE-HEIGHT: normal; TEXT-INDENT: -15.95pt; mso-add-space: auto; mso-list: l2 level1 lfo7"><SPAN

      or energy purchase is no less than 10MW.<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
      <P class=MsoNormal 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: normal"><SPAN

      <P class=MsoNormal

      CLP Group's<o:p></o:p></SPAN></B></P>
      <P class=MsoNormal

    <TD

      storage facilities that are:<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
      <P class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 15.95pt; LINE-HEIGHT: normal; TEXT-INDENT: -15.95pt; mso-add-space: auto; mso-list: l2 level1 lfo7"><SPAN

      owned by CLP or under CLP’s operational control, defined as full authority 
      to implement CLP’s operating policies;<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
      <P class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 15.95pt; LINE-HEIGHT: normal; TEXT-INDENT: -15.95pt; mso-add-space: auto; mso-list: l2 level1 lfo7"><SPAN

      operation during the reporting year; and<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
      <P class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 15.95pt; LINE-HEIGHT: normal; TEXT-INDENT: -15.95pt; mso-add-space: auto; mso-list: l2 level1 lfo7"><SPAN

      material impact to the environment.<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
